The door guarding the entrance to the hag's lair. It's actually transparent and the player can walk through it. It's a cut scene as the door tries to project images onto the player and communicate to them. Pleading with them to leave. The door was a thief that was taken by Ethel and torn to shreds, with the remainder of his body transformed into a door.
